UserData/PatchInfoNewFeatures/1_Patch Notes=Have been fought from RTS to MMO-RPG, and even in a mystical Team Brawler game. Today, he has returned to play RTS games.<n/><n/>Now introduce the 1st Melee AI, in the history of the whloe Mod: <s val="HelpControlsPanelHeader_Terr">Thrall - the Warchief of the Horde</s>.<n/><n/>You can team up with him or fight him as a enemy. For new players of the RTS series, the former option is advised, because of reasons.<n/><n/>As a <s val="HelpControlsPanelHeader_Terr">AI Commander</s>, Thrall plays Orc (of course), and his starting hero is always <s val="HelpControlsPanelHeader_Prot">Far Seer</s> - HIMSELF (it's just a Far Seer skin, all his balance data is the same as the melee Far Seer).<n/><n/>Thrall's secondary hero would be randomly chosen between the <s val="HelpControlsPanelHeader_Prot">Tauren Chieftain</s> and the <s val="HelpControlsPanelHeader_Prot">Shadow Hunter</s> (Why no Blademaster, you ask? Come on, what's the point of using the Blademaster as the 2nd hero in Melee?)<n/><n/>While you are teaming up with Thrall, don't forget to use <s val="HelpControlsPanelHeader_Terr">AI communication</s> <k val="AICommunication" count="1"/> button  to give him instructions - the Warchief is so kindly that instead of executing you in the name of the Horde, he would occasionally listen to you (totally unexpectedly, I know. hail to the Warchief)!<n/><n/><n/><s val="HelpControlsPanelHeader_Prot">Ending Spoiler:</s> After the Thrall AI goes stable, the next big thing of the mod would be a new map - <s val="HelpControlsPanelHeader_Zerg">(4)TurtleRock</s>, which features a Tavern.

UserData/PatchInfoNotes/1_Patch Notes=<s val="HelpControlsPanelHeader_Zerg">Mod Changes</s><n/><ul indent="2" text="•"><li>Thrall AI Online!</li><li>Now you can build on Ramp!</li><li><s val="HelpGameMechanicsPanelHeader_Prot">Ghoul </s>and <s val="HelpGameMechanicsPanelHeader_Prot">Goblin Shredder</s> no longer be count as Army (F4) while they are <s val="HelpGameMechanicsPanelHeader_Zerg">Gathering</s>, and won't be selected by Army Select(F4) button. While non-harvesting ones would be count in the army number, and can be select by F4.</li><li><s val="HelpGameMechanicsPanelHeader_Prot">Mechanical Critter</s> no longer count as Army (F4)</li><li><s val="HelpGameMechanicsPanelHeader_Prot">Blademaster</s>'s <s val="HelpGameMechanicsPanelHeader_Zerg">Bladestorm</s>(Both HD and Non-HD) now get a new visual art.(the official one is broken)</li><li><s val="HelpGameMechanicsPanelHeader_Prot">Spirit Walker</s>'s <s val="HelpGameMechanicsPanelHeader_Zerg">Ethereal </s>form get a new visual art.</li><li>Mind controlled Creeps would no longer try to go back to their original camp.</li><li>Changed <s val="HelpGameMechanicsPanelHeader_Zerg">Human Architecture </s>upgrade to be no longer use triggers, so that map makers could modify it much easier.</li><li>Changed the Higher Ground Missing System to no longer use triggers.</li><li>While attaking from within FoW(e.g. attack a ground unit from higher cliff), the attacker would be fully revealed to the victim (victim would fully gain the vision of the attacking unit), instead of just reveal a snapshot like SC2 does.</li><li>Changed the mechanism of Shock Wave, this ability no use max damage as its limitation instead of max target. (Can potentially hits more targets) </li><li>Optimized the spell:<s val="HelpGameMechanicsPanelHeader_Zerg"> Control Magic</s>.</li><li>Map makers who used this mod can now change the Max damage of the Shock Wave ability via <s val="HelpGameMechanicsPanelText_Terr">Data Editor->User Type->Ability Data - Shock Wave</s></li><li>Map makers who used this mod can now change the Healing Amount of Healing Wave via <s val="HelpGameMechanicsPanelText_Terr">Data Editor->User Type->Ability Data - Healing Wave</s></li><li>Map makers who used this mod can now change the cost fact of Control Magic via <s val="HelpGameMechanicsPanelText_Terr">Data Editor->User Type->Ability Data - Control Magic</s></li><li>Animation of immediately start moving after staring a spell now blends more smoothly (e.g. <s val="HelpGameMechanicsPanelHeader_Prot">Archmage </s>moves immediately after casting <s val="HelpGameMechanicsPanelHeader_Zerg">Summoner Water Element</s>)</li></ul><n/><n/><n/><s val="HelpControlsPanelHeader_Zerg">Bug Fixes</s><n/><ul indent="2" text="•"><n/><li>Fixed a potential leak with the actor: <s val="HelpGameMechanicsPanelText_Terr">War3_SwapableMissileAttackImpactModel</s>.</li><li><s val="HelpGameMechanicsPanelHeader_Zerg">Mass Teleport</s> and <s val="HelpGameMechanicsPanelHeader_Zerg">Scroll of Town Portal</s> would be forcely cancelled if the target dies in the progress.</li><li><s val="HelpGameMechanicsPanelHeader_Prot">Frost Wyrm</s> no longer be considered as 'Powerful Creep'(Immunity to all abilities that can't be used on Heroes).</li><li>Fixed the attacking animation of the <s val="HelpGameMechanicsPanelHeader_Prot">Montain King</s> under <s val="HelpGameMechanicsPanelHeader_Zerg">Avatar </s>form.(It's actually a bug in the official model's animation priory)</li><li>Fixed a issue that make <s val="HelpGameMechanicsPanelHeader_Prot">Dragon Turtle</s>, <s val="HelpGameMechanicsPanelHeader_Prot">Elder Hydra</s>, and <s val="HelpGameMechanicsPanelHeader_Prot">Firelord</s>'s splash damage could destroy items.</li><li>Flyer units no longer have chance to miss while attacking for a lower cliff.</li><li><s val="HelpGameMechanicsPanelHeader_Zerg">Earthquake </s>no longer affects on trees and items.</li><li>While your hero and enmemy hero stand in font of the same non-Netrual shop, the shop would be no longer play annoying sounds.</li></ul>
